        }

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }

          flex-wrap: no-wrap;

        }

          width: 100%;

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Steps to reproduce the problem:



<b class="line"><!---->Steps to reproduce the problem:<!----></b>



<br>





1. First, you need to have a compiled chromium locally



<span class="line"><!---->1. First, you need to have a compiled chromium locally<!----></span>



<br>





2. Run `git apply poc.diff` and recompile chromium locally



<span class="line"><!---->2. Run `git apply poc.diff` and recompile chromium locally<!----></span>



<br>





.What I need to explain here is poc.diff is to trigger the vulnerability function more easily, obviously, it will not maliciously change the program logic



<span class="line"><!---->.What I need to explain here is poc.diff is to trigger the vulnerability function more easily, obviously, it will not maliciously change the program logic<!----></span>



<br>





3. Run `./Chromium.app/Contents/MacOS/Chromium --enable-features=AutofillCreditCardEnabled,AutofillSaveAndFillVPA 



<span class="line"><!---->3. Run `./Chromium.app/Contents/MacOS/Chromium --enable-features=AutofillCreditCardEnabled,AutofillSaveAndFillVPA <!----></span>





http://127.0.0.1:8000/index.html`



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://127.0.0.1:8000/index.html`"><!---->http://127.0.0.1:8000/index.html`<!----></a>





 Click the Submit button, then close the current tab.This is done to free the WebContent object and thus trigger the UAF vulnerability. Note: This is not a vulnerability that can only be triggered by closing the browser.Detailed steps can be reproduced stably following the video.RCA coming soon:)



<span class="line"><!----> Click the Submit button, then close the current tab.This is done to free the WebContent object and thus trigger the UAF vulnerability. Note: This is not a vulnerability that can only be triggered by closing the browser.Detailed steps can be reproduced stably following the video.RCA coming soon:)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

RCA here:



<span class="line"><!---->RCA here:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Very similar to this bug:



<span class="line"><!---->Very similar to this bug:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1240884



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1240884"><!---->https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1240884<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





SaveUPIOfferBubbleViews stores a raw pointer `controller_` to `autofill::SaveUPIBubbleController`. The controller is attached to WebContents and is deleted when the specified WebContents destroyed. However, SaveUPIOfferBubbleViews was not notified when controller being deleted thus a UAF would occur if `controller_` was accessed again.



<span class="line"><!---->SaveUPIOfferBubbleViews stores a raw pointer `controller_` to `autofill::SaveUPIBubbleController`. The controller is attached to WebContents and is deleted when the specified WebContents destroyed. However, SaveUPIOfferBubbleViews was not notified when controller being deleted thus a UAF would occur if `controller_` was accessed again.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The life cycle of class `SaveUPIBubbleControllerImpl` is attached to WebContents,but it failed to inherit from `content::WebContentsObserver` and rewrite `WebContentsDestroyed` function.



<span class="line"><!---->The life cycle of class `SaveUPIBubbleControllerImpl` is attached to WebContents,but it failed to inherit from `content::WebContentsObserver` and rewrite `WebContentsDestroyed` function.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Canary 113.0.5622.0, Dev 113.0.5638.0 and Beta 113.0.5672.24 are affected by this vulnerability.



<span class="line"><!---->Canary 113.0.5622.0, Dev 113.0.5638.0 and Beta 113.0.5672.24 are affected by this vulnerability.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Note:



<span class="line"><!---->Note:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In order to reproduce this vulnerability, we need to execute the following function call chain:



<span class="line"><!---->In order to reproduce this vulnerability, we need to execute the following function call chain:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





FormDataImporter::ImportAndProcessFormData



<span class="line"><!---->FormDataImporter::ImportAndProcessFormData<!----></span>



<br>





	FormDataImporter::ProcessCreditCardImportCandidate



<span class="line"><!---->	FormDataImporter::ProcessCreditCardImportCandidate<!----></span>



<br>





		UpiVpaSaveManager::OfferLocalSave



<span class="line"><!---->		UpiVpaSaveManager::OfferLocalSave<!----></span>



<br>





			ChromeAutofillClient::ConfirmSaveUpiIdLocally



<span class="line"><!---->			ChromeAutofillClient::ConfirmSaveUpiIdLocally<!----></span>



<br>





				SaveUPIBubbleControllerImpl::OfferUpiIdLocalSave



<span class="line"><!---->				SaveUPIBubbleControllerImpl::OfferUpiIdLocalSave<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In this process, the if judgment needs to be satisfied in the FormDataImporter::ProcessCreditCardImportCandidate function:



<span class="line"><!---->In this process, the if judgment needs to be satisfied in the FormDataImporter::ProcessCreditCardImportCandidate function:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





bool FormDataImporter::ProcessCreditCardImportCandidate(



<span class="line"><!---->bool FormDataImporter::ProcessCreditCardImportCandidate(<!----></span>



<br>





    const FormStructure& submitted_form,



<span class="line"><!---->    const FormStructure&amp; submitted_form,<!----></span>



<br>





    const absl::optional<CreditCard>& credit_card_import_candidate,



<span class="line"><!---->    const absl::optional&lt;CreditCard&gt;&amp; credit_card_import_candidate,<!----></span>



<br>





    const absl::optional<std::string>& extracted_upi_id,



<span class="line"><!---->    const absl::optional&lt;std::string&gt;&amp; extracted_upi_id,<!----></span>



<br>





    bool payment_methods_autofill_enabled,



<span class="line"><!---->    bool payment_methods_autofill_enabled,<!----></span>



<br>





    bool is_credit_card_upstream_enabled) {



<span class="line"><!---->    bool is_credit_card_upstream_enabled) {<!----></span>



<br>





#if !BUILDFLAG(IS_ANDROID) && !BUILDFLAG(IS_IOS)



<span class="line"><!---->#if !BUILDFLAG(IS_ANDROID) &amp;&amp; !BUILDFLAG(IS_IOS)<!----></span>



<br>





  if (extracted_upi_id && payment_methods_autofill_enabled &&



<span class="line"><!---->  if (extracted_upi_id &amp;&amp; payment_methods_autofill_enabled &amp;&amp;<!----></span>



<br>





      base::FeatureList::IsEnabled(features::kAutofillSaveAndFillVPA)) {



<span class="line"><!---->      base::FeatureList::IsEnabled(features::kAutofillSaveAndFillVPA)) {<!----></span>



<br>





    upi_vpa_save_manager_->OfferLocalSave(*extracted_upi_id);



<span class="line"><!---->    upi_vpa_save_manager_-&gt;OfferLocalSave(*extracted_upi_id);<!----></span>



<br>





  }



<span class="line"><!---->  }<!----></span>



<br>





#endif



<span class="line"><!---->#endif<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





Therefore, the following flags need to be enabled when reproducing the vulnerability:



<span class="line"><!---->Therefore, the following flags need to be enabled when reproducing the vulnerability:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





--enable-features=AutofillCreditCardEnabled,AutofillSaveAndFillVPA



<span class="line"><!---->--enable-features=AutofillCreditCardEnabled,AutofillSaveAndFillVPA<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





But what puzzles me is that the condition of `extracted_upi_id` is not met all the time. At present, I have not found a way to trigger the call of the `extracted_upi_id` symbol condition, but this is not related to the principle of the vulnerability described above. Therefore, I provide poc.diff to trigger the vulnerability function more conveniently, release the WebContent object and trigger UAF.



<span class="line"><!---->But what puzzles me is that the condition of `extracted_upi_id` is not met all the time. At present, I have not found a way to trigger the call of the `extracted_upi_id` symbol condition, but this is not related to the principle of the vulnerability described above. Therefore, I provide poc.diff to trigger the vulnerability function more conveniently, release the WebContent object and trigger UAF.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Finally, I would like to add a few more details:



<span class="line"><!---->Finally, I would like to add a few more details:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Before the Bisect commit:



<span class="line"><!---->Before the Bisect commit:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/4293475



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/4293475"><!---->https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/4293475<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





The function `SaveUPIOfferBubbleViews::WindowClosing` has not been implemented, which means that although we can make `controller_` a dangling pointer by closing the browser tab, there is no function call that can use this dangling pointer. However the root cause of the vulnerability



<span class="line"><!---->The function `SaveUPIOfferBubbleViews::WindowClosing` has not been implemented, which means that although we can make `controller_` a dangling pointer by closing the browser tab, there is no function call that can use this dangling pointer. However the root cause of the vulnerability<!----></span>



<br>





 is not the addition of the `SaveUPIOfferBubbleViews::WindowClosing` function, but because the life cycle of controller_ and WebContents was not managed well when class SaveUPIOfferBubbleViews、SaveUPIBubbleControllerImpl was first implemented.



<span class="line"><!----> is not the addition of the `SaveUPIOfferBubbleViews::WindowClosing` function, but because the life cycle of controller_ and WebContents was not managed well when class SaveUPIOfferBubbleViews、SaveUPIBubbleControllerImpl was first implemented.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->(putting back Security_Severity because even Security_Impact-None bugs should have severity)<!----></span>

Reporter, thanks for the report! This absolutely will go to the VRP panel for consideration. We do reward bugs even if they're unlaunched features, because we want to incentivize reporters to tell us about bugs _before_ those features ship to users. Obviously I can't promise whether the VRP panel will decide to reward this bug, but it will go to them for consideration.



<span class="line"><!---->Reporter, thanks for the report! This absolutely will go to the VRP panel for consideration. We do reward bugs even if they're unlaunched features, because we want to incentivize reporters to tell us about bugs _before_ those features ship to users. Obviously I can't promise whether the VRP panel will decide to reward this bug, but it will go to them for consideration.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





However, there might be more of a delay than usual. Bugs don't go to the VRP panel until a fix has been landed. As this doesn't currently impact end users, we won't necessarily fix it as quickly as some other bugs. You might have to wait a while. Sorry in advance.



<span class="line"><!---->However, there might be more of a delay than usual. Bugs don't go to the VRP panel until a fix has been landed. As this doesn't currently impact end users, we won't necessarily fix it as quickly as some other bugs. You might have to wait a while. Sorry in advance.<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.<!----></span>

 issue

<h3 class="medium-heading"><!----> issue</h3>


          


            

Target project:

<label for="targetProjectInput">Target project:</label>


            


              

<input id="targetProjectInput" aria-owns="chops-autocomplete-1" aria-autocomplete="both" aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="listbox" aria-activedescendant="">


              




      


        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
